msg:When I came to Nanjing for a trip, I was entangled for a long time about what hotel to stay in, and I also did a lot of research. In the end, I booked the Lalu. I also learned about the Lalu in advance. Just looking at the introduction and publicity, I felt that this hotel was very special. I prefer quietness, and the hotel is located in a relatively secluded location, so it is very suitable for me, especially the bamboo driveway of the hotel is quite special. We are traveling by car, and there are parking spaces at the door, which is very convenient. As soon as I arrived at the hotel door, someone opened the car door and greeted me, helped with the luggage, and was very enthusiastic. As soon as I entered the hotel door, I smelled a faint aroma. When I walked up the stairs, I saw something like a musical instrument. The staff also enthusiastically introduced to us that this is a unique musical instrument of the Lalu: Celadon Ou Music, a very special name, and there will be performances every weekend. Otherwise, it was a coincidence that I happened to catch up with Sunday. After understanding the time, I specially set an alarm clock to remind myself to watch the performance, and then went to the front desk to check in. The ladies at the front desk were all smiling, and I was a little embarrassed by their enthusiasm, haha. As soon as I sat down, they served me hot tea and a towel, and introduced me that this is a special instrument in Taiwan. Color tea: Winter melon tea, especially delicious. I asked if I could pack two cups to take back to the room. The lady immediately packed two cups for me. She was really responsive. After checking in, the front desk lady personally led us to the room, introduced the breakfast time and location, and some leisure and entertainment places in the hotel. We had a lot of fun chatting along the way. When we got to the room, she also introduced in detail how to use some of the equipment in the room, as well as the visiting locations of common items. I can say that few hotels can provide such extreme service, no perfunctory, no impatience, not to cope with work, but to serve every guest happily from the heart. When the guests are happy, they can also feel that they will be happier, so the happy time is always very short, and it is also very reluctant to leave. Before leaving, I specifically asked the names of several front desk ladies who impressed me the most: Pan Zhujie, Yu Jingwen, and guest service manager Sun Yuchen. Of course, I am also very grateful to all the hotel staff who served us with sincerity during our stay. The Lalu is more wonderful because of you! More excellent!

msg:Nanjing Hanbi Tower is a hotel with great cultural and creative characteristics. It is also the third Hanbi Tower hotel in the world.
When you step into the hotel lobby, you will see the celadon Ou music from the Six Dynasties period, as if you can talk to the ancients thousands of years ago by knocking on it. The sound becomes clearer and clearer, they are no longer silent objects, and their agile souls have arisen. The plum tree standing in the middle of the lobby is the tree of life of Bilou. On the wall of the reception area are brick rubbings of portraits of the Seven Sages of the Bamboo Grove.
In the room, the large panoramic floor-to-ceiling windows provide a panoramic view of the Yangtze River, and at dusk, you can even have a panoramic view of the sunset over the Yangtze River. When night falls, it is a pleasure to sip a glass of red wine, taste a piece of pineapple cake, and feel the time in Jinling.
You must come to Nanjing once and stay in Hanbi Tower! Here you can lie in the room and watch the river view, here you can enjoy different delicacies, here you can learn knowledge in the library, here you can appreciate the ancient capital of the Six Dynasties culture!

[Service] 1) Once you make a reservation, you cannot cancel it under any circumstances. Even if you cannot check in, you will not refund it.
